if you're not pregnant , you can take a loan out from us . "	如果沒有懷孕 , 就可以從我們這裡借出貸款 。 」
and that was run by them .	那是由他們來管理的 。
and after 35/36 years , it's still going on .	在35/36年後 , 它仍然在進行中 。
it's a part of the village development bank ; it's not a real bank , but it's a fund microcredit .	這是鄉村發展銀行的一部分 , 不是真的銀行 , 而是一筆基金 。
and we didn't need a big organization to run it it was run by the villagers themselves .	我們不需要一個大型組織來運作 , 而是靠村民自己來運作 。
and you probably hardly see a thai man there , it's always women , women , women , women .	你可能很難在那看到泰國男子那裡 , 永遠都是女人、女人、女人 。
and then we thought we'd help america , because america's been helping everyone , whether they want help or not .	接著 , 我們認為我們會協助美國 , 因為美國一直在協助大家 , 不論他們是否想要協助 。
and this is on the fourth of july .	這張是7月4號
we decided to provide vasectomy to all men , but in particular , american men to the front of the queue , right up to the ambassador's residence during his [unclear] .	我們決定為全國男性提供輸精管切除術 , 特別是 , 排在隊伍前面的美國人 , 直接到大使館去 。
and the hotel gave us the ballroom for it very appropriate room .	飯店給了我們一間交響間 , 非常適當的場所 。
and since it was near lunch time , they said , " all right , we'll give you some lunch .	正因為午餐時間快到了 , 他們說: 「 好吧 , 我們會午餐 。
of course , it must be american cola .	當然 , 它一定是美國的可樂 。
you get two brands , coke and pepsi .	有兩種品牌 , 可口可樂和百事可樂 。
and then the food is either hamburger or hotdog . "	食物是漢堡或熱狗 。 」
and i thought a hotdog will be more symbolic .	我覺得熱狗比較有象徵意義 。
and here is this , then , young man called willy bohm who worked for the usaid .	這位年輕人名叫威利•波姆 , 他為美國國際開發總署工作 。
obviously , he's had his vasectomy because his hotdog is half eaten , and he was very happy .	很顯然 , 他已經做完手術了 , 因為他熱狗的一半被吃掉了 , 他非常開心 。
it made a lot of news in america , and it angered some people also .	這讓美國有很多新聞 , 而且也讓一些人很憤怒 。
i said , " don't worry . come over and i'll do the whole lot of you . "	我說: 「 別擔心 , 過來我會幫你們做很多事 。 」
in all this thing , from seven children to 1 . 5 children , population growth rate of 3 . 3 to 0 . 5 .	總的來說 , 從七個孩子到1.5個孩子 , 人口成長率為3.3到0.5 。
you could call it the cocacola approach if you like it was exactly the same thing .	你可以稱它為可口可樂法 。 如果你喜歡它的話 。
i'm not sure whether cocacola followed us , or we followed cocacola , but we're good friends .	我不確定是可口可樂還是可口可樂 , 但我們是好朋友 。
and so that's the case of everyone joining in .	這就是每個人加入的情況 。
we didn't have a strong government . we didn't have lots of doctors .	我們沒有強大的政府 , 我們沒有很多醫生 。
but it's everybody's job who can change attitude and behavior .	但每個人都有工作可以改變態度和行為 。
then aids came along and hit thailand , and we had to stop doing a lot of good things to fight aids .	接著 , 愛滋病襲擊泰國 , 我們不得不繼續對抗愛滋病做很多好事 。

so i thought , " well , if you can't go to the government , go to the military . "	所以我想: 「 嗯 , 如果你不能去政府 , 去軍隊 。 」
so i went to the military and asked to borrow 300 radio stations .	所以我去拜訪軍方 , 請求借用300個電台 。
they have more than the government , and they've got more guns than the government .	他們擁有的不只是政府 , 而且他們擁有的槍多於政府 。
so i asked them , could they help us in our fight against hiv .	所以我請求他們 , 能否幫我們對抗愛滋病毒 。
and after i gave them statistics , they said , " yes . okay . you can use all the radio stations , television stations . "	我做完統計數字後 , 他們說: 「 是的 。 你可以使用所有的電台、電視台 。 」
and that's when we went onto the airwaves .	那時 , 我們上了 「 空波 」 公司 。

he became the chairman of the national aids committee and increased the budget fiftyfold .	他成為了國立愛滋病委員會的主席 , 並增加了預算金額五倍 。
every ministry , even judges , had to be involved in aids education everyone and we said the public , institutions , religious institutions , schools everyone was involved .	每個部長 , 甚至法官 , 都必須接受愛滋病的教育 , 每一個人我們說 , 公共、機構、宗教機構、學校--每個人都參與其中 。
and here , every media person had to be trained for hiv .	在這裡 , 每個媒體人員都要接受愛滋病毒的訓練 。
and we gave every station half a minute extra for advertising to earn more money .	我們給每一站多餘一分鐘 , 讓廣告能賺更多錢 。
so they were happy with that .	所以他們對此很滿意 。
and then aids education in all schools , starting from university .	所有學校都有愛滋病的教育 , 從大學開始 。
and these are high school kids teaching high school kids .	這些是高中生教導高中生 。
and the best teachers were the girls , not the boys , and they were terrific .	最好的老師是女孩 , 不是男孩 , 他們超棒的 。
and these girls who go around teaching about safe sex and hiv were known as mother theresa .	這些到處教導有關安全性愛和愛滋病毒的女孩 , 被稱為 「 泰瑞莎修女 」 。
and then we went down one more step .	然後我們又往下一步 。
these are primary school kids third , fourth grade going to every household in the village , every household in the whole of thailand , giving aids information and a condom to every household , given by these young kids .	這些是小學三年級的學生 , 四年級 , 拜訪了村子裡的每個家庭 , 泰國的每個家庭 , 提供愛滋病的資訊和保險套 , 給這些孩子提供 。
and no parents objected , because we were trying to save lives , and this was a lifesaver .	沒有任何家長反對 , 因為我們試著拯救生命 , 而這是救生員 。

so you have the companies also realizing that sick staff don't work , and dead customers don't buy .	所以公司也意識到員工生病了 , 消費者不再工作 , 消費者不再買東西 。

and then we gave condoms out everywhere on the streets everywhere , everywhere .	然後我們在街上發放保險套 , 無處不在 。

we had condoms in all the refrigerators in the hotels and the schools , because alcohol impairs judgment .	在旅館和學校的冰箱中 , 我們有保險套 , 因為酒精很容易影響判斷力 。

and then we decided to help people out of poverty , now that we got aids somewhat out of the way this time , not with government alone , but in cooperation with the business community .	接著我們決定要幫助人們脫離貧窮 , 現在我們已經脫離愛滋病的方式 , 這次 , 不只是政府 , 而是和商業社群合作 。
because poor people are business people who lack business skills and access to credit .	因為貧窮的人是商人 , 他們缺乏商業技能 , 無法取得信用 。
those are the things to be provided by the business community .	要提供這些東西給商業社群 。
we're trying to turn them into barefoot entrepreneurs , little business people .	我們試著將這些人轉為赤腳企業家 , 讓他們能做些小生意 。
the only way out of poverty is through business enterprise .	擺脫貧窮的唯一方法 , 就是透過企業 。
so , that was done .	所以 , 完成了 。
the money goes from the company into the village via treeplanting .	公司投入資金 , 從村莊移植到村莊 。

they plant the trees , and the money goes into their microcredit fund , which we call the village development bank .	他們種植樹木 , 金錢就投入到小額貸款基金中 , 也就是鄉村發展銀行 。
everybody joins in , and they feel they own the bank , because they have brought the money in .	每個人加入 , 他們覺得自己擁有銀行 , 因為銀行把錢帶進來 。
and before you can borrow the money , you need to be trained .	在貸款之前 , 你需要接受訓練 。
and we believe if you want to help the poor , those who are living in poverty , access to credit must be a human right .	我們相信如果你想幫助窮人 , 那些生活在貧窮環境的人 , 信用能力就必須要成為一種人權 。
access to credit must be a human right .	信用能力必須是人權 。
otherwise they'll never get out of poverty .	否則他們永遠無法擺脫貧窮 。
and then before getting a loan , you must be trained .	在取得貸款之前 , 必須要先受過訓練 。
here's what we call a " barefoot mba , " teaching people how to do business so that , when they borrow money , they'll succeed with the business .	我們稱之為赤腳mba教導人們如何做生意這樣一來 , 當他們借錢的時候他們就成功了

they said , " they should stop making shoes and clothes .	他們說: 「 不要再做鞋子和衣服了 。
make these better , because we can afford them . "	把這些做得更好 , 因為我們可以負擔得起 。 」

and then now , finally in education , we want to change the school as being underutilized into a place where it's a lifelong learning center for everyone .	最後 , 在教育上 , 我們想要把學校變成一個被充分利用到一個地方 , 在那裡 , 它是每個人的終身學習中心 。

your smartphone may feel like a friend but a true friend would give you a smile once in a while . at ted2013 , keller rinaudo demos romo , the smartphonepowered mini robot who can motor along with you on a walk , slide you a cup of coffee across the table , and react to you with programmable expressions .	你的智慧型手機可能會像是個朋友 , 但有位朋友 , 在ted2013年有一次會給你微笑 , 在凱勒•里納多•羅莫 , 他是智慧型手機的迷你 , 他可以和你一起散步 , 滑動在桌子上喝杯咖啡 , 然後對你做出反應 , 做出可程式化的表情 。
keller rinaudo: a mini robot powered by your phone	kellerrinaudo:一個迷你機器人是由你的手機所驅動 。
so just by a show of hands , how many of you all have a robot at home ?	舉個手 , 你們當中有多少人家裡有機器人 ?
not very many of you .	很多人都不是 。
okay . and actually of those hands , if you don't include roomba how many of you have a robot at home ?	請舉手如果你不包含家裡有機器人你家裡有幾隻機器人 ?
that's the problem that we're trying to solve at romotive that i and the other 20 nerds at romotive are obsessed with solving .	這是我們在romotive努力想辦法解決的問題我和20位宅男在romotive解決的問題 。
so we really want to build a robot that anyone can use , whether you're eight or 80 .	所以我們真的想要打造一個讓任何人都能用的機器人 , 不論你是八歲或八十歲 。
and as it turns out , that's a really hard problem , because you have to build a small , portable robot that's not only really affordable , but it has to be something that people actually want to take home and have around their kids .	事實證明 , 這是個非常困難的問題 , 因為你要做出一個很小、容易攜帶的機器人 , 它不但要能負擔得起 , 還得要真正讓人們想要帶回家 , 並讓孩子擁有它 。
this robot can't be creepy or uncanny .	這種機器人不會很毛骨悚然或不討厭 。
he should be friendly and cute .	他應該要友善又可愛 。
romo's a robot that uses a device you already know and love your iphone as his brain .	romo這個機器人 , 使用一個你已經知道且喜愛你的iphone來做為他的大腦 。
and by leveraging the power of the iphone's processor , we can create a robot that is wifi enabled and computer visioncapable for 150 bucks , which is about one percent of what these kinds of robots have cost in the past .	藉由iphone處理器的力量我們可以創造一個wi-fi無線網路設備的機器人同時擁有電腦視覺能力 , 有150塊美金這大約是過去那種機器人在過去所花費的百分之一

so he's actually using the video camera on the device to follow my face .	所以他其實是在裝置上用攝影機來追蹤我的臉 。
if i duck down , he'll follow me .	如果我蹲下 , 他會跟著我 。
he's wary , so he'll keep his eyes on me .	牠很小心 , 所以牠會一直盯著我 。
if i come over here , he'll turn to follow me .	如果我走到這裡 , 他會轉向跟著我 。
if i come over here he's smart .	如果我過來這裡 , 他很聰明 。
and if i get too close to him , he gets scared just like any other creature .	如果我太靠近他 , 他就會和其他生物一樣害怕 。

so there are all of you through romo's eyes .	透過romo的眼睛 , 你們全部都在那裡 。
and finally , because romo is an extension of me , i can express myself through his emotions .	最後 , 因為romo是我的延伸 , 我可以用他的情緒來表達我自己 。
so i can go in and i can say let's make romo excited .	所以我可以進去 , 說咱們來讓romo興奮一下 。
but the most important thing about romo is that we wanted to create something that was literally completely intuitive .	但關於romo最重要的事是 , 我們想要創造完全直覺的事物 。
you do not have to teach someone how to drive romo .	你不需要教別人如何駕駛romo 。
in fact , who would like to drive a robot ?	事實上 , 有誰想要駕駛機器人 ?
thank you , scott .	謝謝你 , 史考特 。
and even cooler , you actually don't have to be in the same geographic location as the robot to control him .	更酷的是 , 機器人不用在同一個地理位置來控制它 。
so he actually streams twoway audio and video between any two smart devices .	所以他其實是在用任何兩個智能設備之間傳送雙向的音訊和視訊 。
so you can log in through the browser , and it's kind of like skype on wheels .	你可以從瀏覽器登入 , 它有點像輪子上的skype 。
so we were talking before about telepresence , and this is a really cool example .	我們之前談到遠端臨場 , 這是一個很酷的例子 。
you can imagine an eightyearold girl , for example , who has an iphone , and her mom buys her a robot .	你可以想像一個八歲大的女孩 , 她有一支iphone , 而她媽媽買給她一個機器人 。
that girl can take her iphone , put it on the robot , send an email to grandma , who lives on the other side of the country .	那個女孩可以拿著她的iphone , 把它放到機器人上 , 寄給住在國家另一端的祖母 。
grandma can log into that robot and play hideandgoseek with her granddaughter for fifteen minutes every single night , when otherwise she might only be able to get to see her granddaughter once or twice a year .	奶奶可以登入那個機器人 , 和她的孫女一起玩捉迷藏藥 , 每晚十五分鐘 , 否則她一年可能只能一次或兩次見面 。
so those are a couple of the really cool things that romo can do today .	所以這些是romo現今能做的一些很酷的事 。
but i just want to finish by talking about something that we're working on in the future .	但我最後要說的是我們在未來努力的事情 。
this is actually something that one of our engineers , dom , built in a weekend .	這實際上是我們的一個工程師 , dom , 在一個週末完成的 。
it's built on top of a google open framework called blockly .	它是建立在google一個叫做blockly的開放框架上的 。
this allows you to drag and drop these blocks of semantic code and create any behavior for this robot you want .	這可以讓你拖拉這些代碼的積木然後創造任何你想要的機器人的行為 。
you do not have to know how to code to create a behavior for romo .	你不需要知道如何編寫romo的行為 。
and you can actually simulate that behavior in the browser , which is what you see romo doing on the left .	你實際上可以在瀏覽器中模擬這個行為 , 也就是你看到romo在左邊的樣子 。
and then if you have something you like , you can download it onto your robot and execute it in real life , run the program in real life .	如果你有你喜歡的東西 , 你可以下載它到你的機器人 , 並在現實生活中執行它 , 即時執行程式 。
and then if you have something you're proud of , you can share it with every other person who owns a robot in the world .	如果你有什麼可以讓你自豪的話 , 你可以和世界上每個擁有機器人的人分享 。
so all of these wifi–enabled robots actually learn from each other .	所有這些wi-fi無線網路的機器人都能互相學習
the reason we're so focused on building robots that everyone can train is that we think the most compelling use cases in personal robotics are personal .	我們之所以著重在建造一個每個人都可以訓練的機器人 , 是因為我們認為在個人機器人中 , 最吸引人的使用方式是屬於個人的 。
they change from person to person .	它們會從人變成人 。
so we think that if you're going to have a robot in your home , that robot ought to be a manifestation of your own imagination .	所以 , 我們認為 , 如果你在家裡要有個機器人 , 那機器人應該是你想像力的表現 。
so i wish that i could tell you what the future of personal robotics looks like .	我真希望我能告訴你個人機器人的未來是什麼樣子 。
to be honest , i have no idea .	老實說 , 我不知道 。
but what we do know is that it isn't 10 years or 10 billion dollars or a large humanoid robot away .	但我們知道的是 , 它不是十年或一百億美金 , 或一個大型的類人形機器人 。
the future of personal robotics is happening today , and it's going to depend on small , agile robots like romo and the creativity of people like yourselves .	個人機器人的未來發生在今天 , 它取決於小型、敏捷的機器人 , 如romo , 以及像你們一樣的人的創造力 。
so we can't wait to get you all robots , and we can't wait to see what you build .	所以 , 我們不用等待把機器人送上 , 我們也等不及想看看你建造了什麼 。
author and activist isabel allende discusses women , creativity , the definition of feminism and , of course , passion in this talk .	作家和活動家伊莎貝爾•阿言德討論了女性、創意、女性主義的定義 , 當然 , 還有這場演講的熱情 。
entertainment , global issues , love , parenting , storytelling , women , world cultures	娛樂、全球議題、愛、為人父母、講故事、女人、世界文化 ,
isabel allende tells tales of passion	伊莎貝爾•阿言德講述充滿熱情的故事 。
thank you so much . it's really scary to be here among the smartest of the smart .	非常謝謝你 。 來到這裡真的是最聰明的一員 。
i'm here to tell you a few tales of passion .	我在這裡要告訴各位幾個關於熱情的故事 。
there's a jewish saying that i love .	我愛這句猶太諺語 。
what is truer than truth ? answer: the story .	比事實更真誠的是什麼 ? 答案:故事 。
i'm a storyteller . i want to convey something that is truer than truth about our common humanity .	我是說故事的人 。 我想傳達一些比我們共同的人性真實的東西 。
all stories interest me , and some haunt me until i end up writing them .	我對所有故事都感興趣 , 有些則令我不安直到我最後寫完它們 。
certain themes keep coming up: justice , loyalty , violence , death , political and social issues , freedom .	有些主題不斷出現正義、忠誠、暴力、死亡、政治和社會議題、自由 。
i'm aware of the mystery around us , so i write about coincidences , premonitions , emotions , dreams , the power of nature , magic .	我意識到我們身邊的難解之事所以我書寫巧合、預兆感情、夢想大自然的力量、魔法
in the last 20 years i have published a few books , but i have lived in anonymity until february of 2006 , when i carried the olympic flag in the winter olympics in italy .	在過去的20年裡 , 我出版了幾本書 , 但我一直住在匿名性 , 直到2006年2月 , 我帶著義大利冬季奧運的奧運旗幟 。
that made me a celebrity . now people recognize me in macy's , and my grandchildren think that i'm cool .	這讓我成為了名人 。 現在 , 大家在梅西百貨上認識我 , 我的孫子認為我很酷 。
allow me to tell you about my four minutes of fame .	讓我告訴你我四分鐘的名氣 。
one of the organizers of the olympic ceremony , of the opening ceremony , called me and said that i had been selected to be one of the flagbearers .	一名籌辦奧運開幕式的籌辦人打電話給我 , 說我被選為旗手之一 。
i replied that surely this was a case of mistaken identity because i'm as far as you can get from being an athlete .	我回答 , 這是個錯誤認同的案例因為我可以從運動員的角度取得 。
actually , i wasn't even sure that i could go around the stadium without a walker .	事實上 , 我甚至不確定可以不用助行器就能在體育場四周走動 。
i was told that this was no laughing matter .	我被告知這不是開心的事 。
this would be the first time that only women would carry the olympic flag .	這是第一次 , 只有女性會帶著奧運國旗 。
five women , representing five continents , and three olympic gold medal winners .	五位女性代表五大洲以及三位奧林匹克獎得主
my first question was , naturally , what was i going to wear ?	很自然地 , 我的第一個問題是:我要穿什麼 ?
a uniform , she said , and asked for my measurements .	她說 , 一件制服 , 要求我的測量標準 。
i had a vision of myself in a fluffy anorak , looking like the michelin man .	我有個景象 , 彷彿自己處在富裕的主流之中 , 看起來像米其林人 。
by the middle of february , i found myself in turin , where enthusiastic crowds cheered when any of the 80 olympic teams was in the street .	到了二月中期 , 我到了杜林 , 那裡有熱情的群眾在街上為80個奧運隊加油 。
those athletes had sacrificed everything to compete in the games .	那些運動員為了競爭而犧牲了一切 。
they all deserved to win , but there's the element of luck .	他們都有贏的權利 , 但還是有運氣的要素 。
a speck of snow , an inch of ice , the force of the wind , can determine the result of a race or a game .	雪上的小東西 , 冰的一英吋 , 風的力量 , 可以決定比賽的結果 。
however , what matters most more than training or luck is the heart .	然而 , 訓練或運氣之外 , 最重要的因素就是心 。
only a fearless and determined heart will get the gold medal .	只有無懼且堅定的心才能得到金牌 。
it is all about passion .	重點都在於熱情 。
the streets of turin were covered with red posters announcing the slogan of the olympics .	杜林街上滿是紅色海報 , 宣佈奧運的口號 。
passion lives here . isn't it always true ?	熱情就在這裡 。 不是總是如此嗎 ?
heart is what drives us and determines our fate .	心 , 是我們的動力 , 決定我們的命運 。
that is what i need for my characters in my books: a passionate heart .	這就是我在書中角色所需要的:熱情的心 。
i need mavericks , dissidents , adventurers , outsiders and rebels , who ask questions , bend the rules and take risks .	我需要充滿反骨、異議、勇於冒險、冒險精神、外來者和叛軍 , 他們提出質疑、調整規則 , 並勇於冒險 。
people like all of you in this room .	就像在座各位
nice people with common sense do not make interesting characters .	普通感官的好人不會是有趣的角色 。
they only make good former spouses .	他們只會交配好的前夫 。
in the green room of the stadium , i met the other flag bearers: three athletes , and the actresses susan sarandon and sophia loren .	在體育場的綠色房間裡 , 我見到其他旗手三位運動員 , 演員蘇珊莎蘭登和蘇菲雅羅蘭 。
also , two women with passionate hearts: wangari maathai , the nobel prizewinner from kenya who has planted 30 million trees . and by doing so , she has changed the soil , the weather , in some places in africa , and of course the economic conditions in many villages .	另外 , 兩個有熱忱心心心的女人來自肯亞的諾貝爾獎得主她種了三千萬棵樹 。 透過這麼做 , 她改變了土壤 , 在非洲的某些地方 , 當然也改變了許多村落的經濟狀況 。
and somaly mam , a cambodian activist who fights passionately against child prostitution .	柬埔寨行動主義者索馬利•瑪曼 , 極力對抗兒童妓女 。
when she was 14 years old , her grandfather sold her to a brothel .	當她十四歲時 , 她的祖父將她賣到妓院 。
she told us of little girls raped by men who believe that having sex with a very young virgin will cure them from aids .	她告訴我們 , 小女孩被男人強暴那些人相信跟非常年輕的處女做愛可以治癒愛滋病
and of brothels where children are forced to receive five , 15 clients per day , and if they rebel , they are tortured with electricity .	還有那些每天被迫接收五、十五名客戶的妓院 , 如果他們反抗 , 他們會被電擊折磨 。
in the green room i received my uniform .	在綠色房間 , 我收到制服 。
it was not the kind of outfit that i normally wear , but it was far from the michelin man suit that i had anticipated . not bad , really .	這不是我平常穿的衣服 , 但那不是我所預期的米其林男人裝的衣服 , 真的不糟 。
i looked like a refrigerator .	我看起來像冰箱 。
but so did most of the flagbearers , except sophia loren , the universal symbol of beauty and passion .	但也有大部分的旗幟 , 除了蘇菲雅羅蘭這種普遍的美麗和熱情的象徵
sophia is over 70 and she looks great .	蘇菲雅七十多歲 , 她看起來很棒 。
she's sexy , slim and tall , with a deep tan .	她很性感 , 很瘦 , 又很高 , 帶著很深的棕色 。
now , how can you have a deep tan and have no wrinkles ?	那麼 , 你要如何有深色的皮膚和沒有皺紋 ?
when asked in a tv interview , " how could she look so good ? "	當電視記者問: 「 她看起來怎麼那麼棒 ? 」
she replied , " posture . my back is always straight , and i don't make old people's noises . "	她回答: 「 姿勢 。 我的背永遠是直的 , 我不會製造老人的噪音 。 」
so , there you have some free advice from one of the most beautiful women on earth .	所以 , 這裡你有一些免費的建議 , 來自地球上最美麗的女人之一 。
no grunting , no coughing , no wheezing , no talking to yourselves , no farting .	不屈不撓、不咳嗽、不貪叫、不跟自己說話、不放屁 。
well , she didn't say that exactly .	嗯 , 她並沒有說真的 。
at some point around midnight , we were summoned to the wings of the stadium , and the loudspeakers announced the olympic flag , and the music started by the way , the same music that starts here , the aida march .	到了午夜的時候 , 我們被叫到體育場的翅膀 , 擴音器負責宣佈奧運旗 , 音樂是從這兒開始的 , 艾達遊行 。
sophia loren was right in front of me she's a foot taller than i am , not counting the poofy hair .	蘇菲雅羅蘭就在我前面 , 她比我高一英呎 , 不算有頭髮 。
she walked elegantly , like a giraffe on the african savannah , holding the flag on her shoulder . i jogged behind on my tiptoes holding the flag on my extended arm , so that my head was actually under the damn flag .	她優雅地走著 , 就像非洲大草原上的長頸鹿 , 肩上拿著旗子 。 我在後面慢跑 , 手臂上拿著旗子 , 所以我的頭其實是在那面該死的旗子下 。
all the cameras were , of course , on sophia .	所有的相機都是蘇菲雅
that was fortunate for me , because in most press photos i appear too , although often between sophia's legs .	這對我來說很幸運 , 因為在大部分媒體照片中我看起來也一樣 , 雖然常在蘇菲雅的雙腿間 。
a place where most men would love to be .	大部分男人會喜歡去的地方 。
the best four minutes of my entire life were those in the olympic stadium .	我一生中最棒的四分鐘是在奧林匹克體育館 。
my husband is offended when i say this although i have explained to him that what we do in private usually takes less than four minutes so he shouldn't take it personally .	我老公覺得被冒犯了──雖然我跟他解釋說 , 我們在私下做的事通常會花不到四分鐘 , 所以他不該把它當做自己 。
i have all the press clippings of those four magnificent minutes , because i don't want to forget them when old age destroys my brain cells .	我有這四分鐘的所有剪報因為我不想在老的時候忘記他們
i want to carry in my heart forever the key word of the olympics passion .	我想要永遠將奧運的關鍵字融入其中 。
so here's a tale of passion .	熱情的故事如下 。
the year is 1998 , the place is a prison camp for tutsi refugees in congo .	1998年 , 剛果的圖西族難民營位於1998年 。
by the way , 80 percent of all refugees and displaced people in the world are women and girls .	順便說一下 , 世界上80%的難民和流離失所者都是女人和女孩 。
we can call this place in congo a death camp , because those who are not killed will die of disease or starvation .	我們可以稱這個地方為剛果的死囚營 , 因為沒有被殺的人 , 會死於疾病或飢餓 。
the protagonists of this story are a young woman , rose mapendo , and her children .	故事的主角是一位年輕女子 , 蘿絲•瑪班多 , 以及她的孩子 。
she's pregnant and a widow .	她是懷孕的寡婦 。
soldiers have forced her to watch as her husband was tortured and killed .	士兵迫使她看著她的丈夫被虐待和殺害 。
somehow she manages to keep her seven children alive , and a few months later , she gives birth to premature twins .	不知何故 , 她讓她七個孩子活著 , 幾個月後 , 她生下早產雙胞胎 。
two tiny little boys .	兩個小男孩 。
she cuts the umbilical cord with a stick , and ties it with her own hair .	她用棍子切割臍帶然後用頭髮綁起來
she names the twins after the camp's commanders to gain their favor , and feeds them with black tea because her milk cannot sustain them .	她用營地指揮官的名字來命名雙胞胎 , 以取得他們的喜好 , 並用黑色茶餵給他們 , 因為她的母乳無法維持它們 。
when the soldiers burst in her cell to rape her oldest daughter , she grabs hold of her and refuses to let go , even when they hold a gun to her head .	當軍人闖進她的牢房 , 強暴她大女兒時 , 她不願意放手 , 即使他們手上拿著槍 。
somehow , the family survives for 16 months , and then , by extraordinary luck , and the passionate heart of a young american man , sasha chanoff , who manages to put her in a u . s . rescue plane , rose mapendo and her nine children end up in phoenix , arizona , where they're now living and thriving .	不知怎麼的 , 這家人存活了十六個月然後 , 靠著絕佳的運氣和熱情的美國人沙夏•查諾夫這家人成功地將她送進美國救援機場蘿絲•瑪班多和九個孩子最後到了亞利桑那州鳳凰城在那裡生活、茁壯成長
mapendo , in swahili , means great love .	瑪班多在斯瓦希里語中代表著偉大的愛 。
the protagonists of my books are strong and passionate women like rose mapendo .	我書中的主角是堅強且充滿熱情的女性 , 像是蘿絲•瑪班多 。
i don't make them up . there's no need for that .	我不編造它們 , 不需要它們 。
i look around and i see them everywhere .	我環顧四周 , 到處都能看到 。
i have worked with women and for women all my life .	我一生都在為女性、為女性工作 。
i know them well .	我對他們很熟悉 。
i was born in ancient times , at the end of the world , in a patriarchal catholic and conservative family .	我出生在一個原始的天主教和保守家庭 。
no wonder that by age five i was a raging feminist although the term had not reached chile yet , so nobody knew what the heck was wrong with me .	難怪我五歲就已經是個憤怒的女權主義者 , 雖然還沒有達到智利 , 所以沒有人知道我到底是怎麼搞的 。
i would soon find out that there was a high price to pay for my freedom , and for questioning the patriarchy .	很快的 , 我就發現要為我的自由付出極大的代價 , 也因為質疑父權主義 。
but i was happy to pay it , because for every blow that i received , i was able to deliver two .	但是我很高興能付出代價 , 因為每當我被擊中的一擊 , 我就能夠分出兩次 。
once , when my daughter paula was in her twenties , she said to me that feminism was dated , that i should move on .	有一次 , 當我的女兒寶拉二十多歲時 , 她對我說 , 女權運動過時了 , 我應該要繼續走下去 。
we had a memorable fight . feminism is dated ?	我們打了一場難忘的仗 。 女權主義約會了嗎 ?
yes , for privileged women like my daughter and all of us here today , but not for most of our sisters in the rest of the world who are still forced into premature marriage , prostitution , forced labor they have children that they don't want or they cannot feed .	是的 , 對於我女兒和在座各位這些有特權的女性來說 , 現今在世界上大多數的姊妹不被迫提早婚姻、妓女、強迫的勞工 , 他們的孩子不想要或他們無法餵食 。
they have no control over their bodies or their lives .	他們無法掌控自己的身體或生活 。
they have no education and no freedom .	他們沒有教育 , 沒有自由 。
they are raped , beaten up and sometimes killed with impunity .	他們被強暴、毆打 , 有時被懲罰 。
for most western young women of today , being called a feminist is an insult .	對於現今大部分西方女性來說 , 被稱為女性主義者是一種侮辱 。
feminism has never been sexy , but let me assure you that it never stopped me from flirting , and i have seldom suffered from lack of men .	女權從來就不吸引人 , 但讓我告訴你 , 我永遠不會因調情而停止自己 , 我也不會因缺乏男人而遭到折磨 。
feminism is not dead , by no means .	女權主義已經死去 , 絕非死 。
it has evolved . if you don't like the term , change it , for goddess' sake .	它已進化 。 如果你不喜歡這個名詞 , 改變它 , 為了女神的天性 。
call it aphrodite , or venus , or bimbo , or whatever you want ; the name doesn't matter , as long as we understand what it is about , and we support it .	稱它為 「 愛芙羅蒂 」 、 「 維納斯 」 、 「 金寶 」 , 或 「 你想不想要的名字 , 只要我們了解它是什麼 , 就可以支持它 。
so here's another tale of passion , and this is a sad one .	這裡還有另一個充滿熱情的故事 , 一個悲傷的故事 。
the place is a small women's clinic in a village in bangladesh .	孟加拉的一個村落是一間婦女診所
the year is 2005 .	時間是2005年 。
jenny is a young american dental hygienist who has gone to the clinic as a volunteer during her threeweek vacation .	珍妮是一位年輕的美國牙醫師她到診所當義工在她三週的假期裡
she's prepared to clean teeth , but when she gets there , she finds out that there are no doctors , no dentists , and the clinic is just a hut full of flies .	她準備好要乾淨的牙齒 , 但當她到達時 , 她發現沒有醫生 , 沒有牙醫 , 而診所只是一間蒼蠅的小屋 。
outside , there is a line of women who have waited several hours to be treated .	外頭有一排女子等了幾個小時才被治療 。
the first patient is in excruciating pain because she has several rotten molars .	第一位病人痛苦難當 , 因為她有好幾顆壞蚊子 。
jenny realizes that the only solution is to pull out the bad teeth .	珍妮知道唯一的辦法就是拔掉壞牙齒 。
she's not licensed for that ; she has never done it .	她沒有執照 , 也從來沒有做過 。
she risks a lot and she's terrified .	她很常冒險 , 她很害怕 。
she doesn't even have the proper instruments , but fortunately she has brought some novocaine .	她甚至沒有合適的樂器 , 但幸運的是 , 她帶來了一些無風琴 。
jenny has a brave and passionate heart .	珍妮有顆勇敢且熱情的心 。
she murmurs a prayer and she goes ahead with the operation .	她不斷祈禱 , 並且開始行動 。
at the end , the relieved patient kisses her hands .	最後 , 病人鬆了口氣吻了她的手 。
that day the hygienist pulls out many more teeth .	那天 , 衛生學家抽出更多的牙齒 。
the next morning , when she comes again to the socalled clinic , her first patient is waiting for her with her husband .	隔天早上 , 當她再次進到所謂的診所時 , 她的第一位病人跟她先生在等她 。
the woman's face looks like a watermelon .	這位女士的臉像個西瓜一樣 。
it is so swollen that you can't even see the eyes .	腫到看不見眼睛
the husband , furious , threatens to kill the american .	丈夫感到憤怒、威脅要殺美國人 。
jenny is horrified at what she has done , but then the translator explains that the patient's condition has nothing to do with the operation .	珍妮對於她做了什麼事嚇壞了 , 但翻譯解釋說病人的狀況和手術沒什麼關係 。
the day before , her husband beat her up because she was not home in time to prepare dinner for him .	前一天 , 她的丈夫打她一頓 , 因為她那時無法準備晚餐給他 。
millions of women live like this today .	現今有數百萬女性過著這樣的生活 。
they are the poorest of the poor .	他們是最貧窮的人 。
although women do twothirds of the world's labor , they own less than one percent of the world's assets .	雖然全世界的勞動力中有三分之二是女性 , 但她們的產量只有不到1% 。
they are paid less than men for the same work if they're paid at all , and they remain vulnerable because they have no economic independence , and they are constantly threatened by exploitation , violence and abuse .	他們的薪水是相同的 , 如果他們有薪水 , 他們會保持脆弱 , 因為他們沒有經濟獨立 , 他們會經常受到剝削、暴力和虐待的威脅 。
it is a fact that giving women education , work , the ability to control their own income , inherit and own property , benefits the society .	這個事實就是 , 給予婦女教育、工作、控制自己收入的能力、繼承和財產的能力 , 讓社會受益 。
if a woman is empowered , her children and her family will be better off .	如果女人有力量 , 她的孩子和她的家庭會變得更好 。
if families prosper , the village prospers , and eventually so does the whole country .	如果家屬富足 , 村落就會繁榮 , 最終整個國家也是 。
wangari maathai goes to a village in kenya .	旺加里•瑪塔伊到肯亞的一個村落
she talks with the women and explains that the land is barren because they have cut and sold the trees .	她跟女人談 , 解釋說土地很貧瘠 , 因為他們砍樹並賣樹木 。
she gets the women to plant new trees and water them , drop by drop .	她讓婦女們種植新樹並澆水 , 一滴接著一滴 。
in a matter of five or six years , they have a forest , the soil is enriched , and the village is saved .	在五六年左右 , 他們有一座森林 , 土壤被豐富 , 而村落就被拯救了 。
the poorest and most backward societies are always those that put women down .	最貧窮和最落後的社會往往就是那些壓抑女性的社會 。
yet this obvious truth is ignored by governments and also by philanthropy .	但這個顯而易見的事實卻被政府以及慈善機構忽略 。
for every dollar given to a women's program , 20 dollars are given to men's programs .	女性的專案每得到1美元就有20美元是男性專案的
women are 51 percent of humankind .	女性是51%的人類 。
empowering them will change everything more than technology and design and entertainment .	給予她們力量 , 不只是科技、設計和娛樂 , 更能改變一切 。
i can promise you that women working together linked , informed and educated can bring peace and prosperity to this forsaken planet .	我可以保證 , 女性可以一起合作連結、有知識、受教育 , 能為這個可怕的星球帶來和平和和繁榮 。
in any war today , most of the casualties are civilians , mainly women and children . they are collateral damage .	在今天的任何一場戰爭中 , 死傷是平民 , 主要是婦女和兒童 , 他們是附帶損傷 。
men run the world , and look at the mess we have .	男人掌控世界 , 看看我們有什麼麻煩 。
what kind of world do we want ?	我們想要什麼樣的世界 ?
this is a fundamental question that most of us are asking .	這是大部分人所問的基本問題 。
does it make sense to participate in the existing world order ?	參與現有的世界秩序合理嗎 ?
we want a world where life is preserved and the quality of life is enriched for everybody , not only for the privileged .	我們想要一個世界 , 在這個世界中 , 生活品質被保存下來 , 且人人的生活品質也被豐富 , 不只是因為特權而被豐富 。
in january i saw an exhibit of fernando botero's paintings at the uc berkeley library .	一月時 , 我看到費南多•巴特羅在加州大學柏克萊圖書館的畫作展示 。
no museum or gallery in the united states , except for the new york gallery that carries botero's work , has dared to show the paintings because the theme is the abu ghraib prison .	在美國 , 沒有任何博物館或畫廊只有紐約畫廊有波特羅的作品勇敢展示這些畫因為主題是阿布格萊布監獄
they are huge paintings of torture and abuse of power , in the voluminous botero style .	它們是大量的酷刑和權力濫用畫作 , 用的是大量的巴特羅風格 。
i have not been able to get those images out of my mind or my heart .	我無法將那些影像從我心中或我的心中移除 。
what i fear most is power with impunity .	我最害怕的是權力和罪犯 。
i fear abuse of power , and the power to abuse .	我害怕濫用權力 , 以及濫用權力 。
in our species , the alpha males define reality , and force the rest of the pack to accept that reality and follow the rules .	在我們這個物種 , 雄性領袖定義現實 , 並迫使其餘的群體接受現實 , 並遵循規則 。
the rules change all the time , but they always benefit them , and in this case , the trickledown effect , which does not work in economics , works perfectly .	規則隨時在改變 , 但總是有好處 , 在這種情況下 , 下滲經濟失敗的效應 , 並沒有效果很好 。
abuse trickles down from the top of the ladder to the bottom .	從上到下都是虐待行為 。
women and children , especially the poor , are at the bottom .	女人和小孩 , 尤其是窮人 , 都在最底層 。
even the most destitute of men have someone they can abuse a woman or a child .	即使是最陰鬱的男人也有人可以虐待女人或小孩 。
i'm fed up with the power that a few exert over the many through gender , income , race , and class .	我受夠了少數人操縱多數人的權力 , 包括性別、收入、種族 , 和階級 。
i think that the time is ripe to make fundamental changes in our civilization .	我認為 , 該是時候成熟 , 讓我們的文明發生根本改變的時候了 。
but for real change , we need feminine energy in the management of the world .	但若要真正改變 , 我們需要讓女性能量在世界的管理之中 。
we need a critical number of women in positions of power , and we need to nurture the feminine energy in men .	我們需要讓女性掌握權力我們需要培養男性心中的女性能量
i'm talking about men with young minds , of course .	當然 , 我指的是有年輕心智的男人 。
old guys are hopeless ; we have to wait for them to die off .	老傢伙是絕望的 ; 我們必須等著他們死去 。
yes , i would love to have sophia loren's long legs and legendary breasts .	是的 , 我很希望蘇菲雅羅蘭的長腿和著名的胸部 。
but given a choice , i would rather have the warrior hearts of wangari maathai , somaly mam , jenny and rose mapendo .	但如果可以選擇 , 我寧願有顆勇敢的心 , 來自旺加里•瑪太、索瑪利•曼、珍妮 , 和蘿絲•瑪班多 。
i want to make this world good .	我想要讓這個世界更美好 。
not better , but to make it good .	不好 , 但要把它做好 。
why not ? it is possible . look around in this room all this knowledge , energy , talent and technology .	為甚麼不呢 ? 這是有可能的 。 看看這房間裡所有這些知識 , 能源 , 人才和科技 。
let's get off our fannies , roll up our sleeves and get to work , passionately , in creating an almost perfect world .	讓我們擺脫冷氣 , 捲起袖子 , 積極地工作 , 創造一個近乎完美的世界 。
every day , in a city the size of london , 30 million meals are served . but where does all the food come from ? architect carolyn steel discusses the daily miracle of feeding a city , and shows how ancient food routes shaped the modern world .	每天 , 在倫敦這麼大的城市 , 有三千萬份餐被供應 。 但 , 所有食物都來自何方 ? 建築師卡洛琳鋼討論到每天供給城市的奇蹟 , 顯示出古老的食物路線如何塑造現代世界 。
cities , culture , food , global issues	城市、文化、食物、全球議題 ,
carolyn steel: how food shapes our cities	碳鋼鐵:食物是如何塑造我們的城市的 ?
how do you feed a city ?	要如何餵飽一座城市 ?
it's one of the great questions of our time .	這是我們這個時代的一個大問題 。
yet it's one that's rarely asked .	但很少被提起 。
we take it for granted that if we go into a shop or restaurant , or indeed into this theater's foyer in about an hour's time , there is going to be food there waiting for us , having magically come from somewhere .	我們視之為理所當然 , 如果我們去商店或餐廳 , 或在一個小時內進入劇院大廳 , 就會有食物在那等著我們 , 神奇地從某個地方來 。
but when you think that every day for a city the size of london , enough food has to be produced , transported , bought and sold , cooked , eaten , disposed of , and that something similar has to happen every day for every city on earth , it's remarkable that cities get fed at all .	但當你想到倫敦這麼大的城市 , 每天要有足夠的食物被製造、運輸、購買、賣、吃、處置同樣的事 , 每天都發生在每個城市 , 都市被餵食是很了不起的 。
we live in places like this as if they're the most natural things in the world , forgetting that because we're animals and that we need to eat , we're actually as dependent on the natural world as our ancient ancestors were .	我們住在這樣的地方 , 就好像他們是世界上最自然的地方 , 忘記了我們是動物 , 我們也需要進食 , 我們也同樣仰賴自然世界 , 就像我們古老的祖先一樣 。
and as more of us move into cities , more of that natural world is being transformed into extraordinary landscapes like the one behind me it's soybean fields in mato grosso in brazil in order to feed us .	隨著更多人搬到城市裡 , 更多的大自然被轉變為非凡的景觀 , 就像我身後的景色--是在巴西馬托格羅索的大豆田 , 為了餵飽我們 。
these are extraordinary landscapes , but few of us ever get to see them .	這些是非凡的景觀 , 但很少人見過它們 。
and increasingly these landscapes are not just feeding us either .	越來越多這樣的景觀不僅僅是用來餵飽我們的食物 。
as more of us move into cities , more of us are eating meat , so that a third of the annual grain crop globally now gets fed to animals rather than to us human animals .	越多人搬到城市裡 , 我們越是吃肉 , 所以每年全球有三分之一的穀物被餵給動物 , 而不是餵給我們人類 。
and given that it takes three times as much grain actually ten times as much grain to feed a human if it's passed through an animal first , that's not a very efficient way of feeding us .	由於它需要三倍的穀物實際上是十倍的穀物如果用動物首先通過 , 餵飽人類的糧食絕對不是個非常有效的方法
and it's an escalating problem too .	這也是個逐步的問題 。
by 2050 , it's estimated that twice the number of us are going to be living in cities .	到2050年 , 估計將是我們在城市中生活的兩倍 。
and it's also estimated that there is going to be twice as much meat and dairy consumed .	據估計 , 肉類和乳製品的消耗量會是兩倍 。
so meat and urbanism are rising hand in hand .	所以 , 都市化和肉的關聯性正逐漸增加 。
and that's going to pose an enormous problem .	這將是個巨大的問題 。
six billion hungry carnivores to feed , by 2050 .	到2050年 , 六十億個肚子要餵食 。
that's a big problem . and actually if we carry on as we are , it's a problem we're very unlikely to be able to solve .	這是個大問題 。 但事實上 , 如果我們繼續這樣下去 , 這是個問題 , 我們不太可能解決 。
nineteen million hectares of rainforest are lost every year to create new arable land .	每年有一千九百萬公頃的熱帶雨林消失 , 被用來創造新的耕地 。
although at the same time we're losing an equivalent amount of existing arables to salinization and erosion .	雖然同時我們也失去同樣數量的可耕地 , 可耕種 , 可耕種 , 可耕種 。
we're very hungry for fossil fuels too .	我們也很渴望化石燃料 。
it takes about 10 calories to produce every calorie of food that we consume in the west .	西方每消費一卡路里的食物要耗費大約十卡路里的能量 。
and even though there is food that we are producing at great cost , we don't actually value it .	即使有很大的成本生產的食物 , 我們卻不珍視它 。
half the food produced in the usa is currently thrown away .	半數在美國生產的食物都被浪費掉了 。
and to end all of this , at the end of this long process , we're not even managing to feed the planet properly .	在這一切的最後 , 在這個過程中 , 我們甚至沒有辦法妥善供應食物 。
a billion of us are obese , while a further billion starve .	有十億人過胖 , 卻又有十億人挨餓 。
none of it makes very much sense .	這一切都不合理 。
and when you think that 80 percent of global trade in food now is controlled by just five multinational corporations , it's a grim picture .	試想全球百分之八十的食物交易只掌控了五大跨國公司 , 這真是可怕的照片 。
as we're moving into cities , the world is also embracing a western diet .	隨著我們搬到城市裡 , 世界也接受了西方飲食習慣 。
and if we look to the future , it's an unsustainable diet .	如果我們看向未來 , 它是種不永續的飲食 。
so how did we get here ?	我們是怎麼走到這一步的 ?
and more importantly , what are we going to do about it ?	更重要的是 , 我們打算怎麼做 ?
well , to answer the slightly easier question first , about 10 , 000 years ago , i would say , is the beginning of this process in the ancient near east , known as the fertile crescent .	第一個問題稍微容易些大概一萬年前 , 我會說是這個過程的開始在古老的近東被稱作 " 新月沃土 "
because , as you can see , it was crescent shaped .	因為 , 如你所見 , 它是月亮的形狀 。
and it was also fertile .	而且還很肥沃 。
and it was here , about 10 , 000 years ago , that two extraordinary inventions , agriculture and urbanism , happened roughly in the same place and at the same time .	大約在一萬年前 , 在這裡有兩項非凡的發明農業和城市的產生大約在同一個地方同時發生
this is no accident , because agriculture and cities are bound together . they need each other .	這不是巧合 , 因為農業和城市是結合在一起的 。 他們彼此需要 。
because it was discovery of grain by our ancient ancestors for the first time that produced a food source that was large enough and stable enough to support permanent settlements .	因為這是我們第一次發現穀物 , 原始祖先就生產出足夠大、穩定的食物來源 , 足以維持永久居住 。
and if we look at what those settlements were like , we see they were compact .	如果我們看看這些聚落是什麼樣子 , 我們可以看到它們是緊密的 。
they were surrounded by productive farm land and dominated by large temple complexes like this one at ur , that were , in fact , effectively , spiritualized , central food distribution centers .	農場的周圍都是有生產力的農地 , 由大型神廟的神殿主宰 , 像是這一個在烏爾的神殿 , 實際上是精神分配中心 。
because it was the temples that organized the harvest , gathered in the grain , offered it to the gods , and then offered the grain that the gods didn't eat back to the people .	因爲是神殿安排收割收集穀物獻給諸神再把上帝吃掉的穀物卻不讓神吃掉
so , if you like , the whole spiritual and physical life of these cities was dominated by the grain and the harvest that sustained them .	所以 , 如果你們願意 , 這些城市的精神和實體生活是由他們賴以生存的穀物和收穫所主宰 。
and in fact , that's true of every ancient city .	事實上 , 每個古老的城市都是如此 。
but of course not all of them were that small .	當然 , 它們不是全部都那麼小 。
famously , rome had about a million citizens by the first century a . d .	眾所皆知 , 在西元一世紀時 , 羅馬就有大約一百萬個公民 。
so how did a city like this feed itself ?	那麼 , 像這樣的城市是怎麼來的 ?
the answer is what i call " ancient food miles . "	答案是 , 我稱之為 「 古老的食物里程 」 。
basically , rome had access to the sea , which made it possible for it to import food from a very long way away .	基本上 , 羅馬可以到海上 , 這讓海草可以從很遠很遠的地方運來進口 。
this is the only way it was possible to do this in the ancient world , because it was very difficult to transport food over roads , which were rough .	這是唯一能做這件事的方式 , 在古代世界中 , 因為要把食物運送到比公路上是非常困難的 , 這很不容易 。
and the food obviously went off very quickly .	食物顯然很快就消失了
so rome effectively waged war on places like carthage and egypt just to get its paws on their grain reserves .	所以羅馬有效地攻擊戰爭 , 如汽車業和埃及 , 若要取得他們的儲備量 , 就能讓戰爭發生 。
and , in fact , you could say that the expansion of the empire was really sort of one long , drawn out militarized shopping spree , really .	事實上 , 你可以說這個帝國的擴張其實是從軍事化的 「 大軍購物中心 」 來的 。
in fact i love the fact , i just have to mention this: rome in fact used to import oysters from london , at one stage . i think that's extraordinary .	事實上 , 我很喜歡這個事實 , 我只需要提到羅馬還曾經從倫敦輸入牡蠣我覺得這很特別
so rome shaped its hinterland through its appetite .	所以羅馬就從食材中塑造它的內陸 。
but the interesting thing is that the other thing also happened in the preindustrial world .	但有趣的是 , 另一個工業界也發生了 。
if we look at a map of london in the 17th century , we can see that its grain , which is coming in from the thames , along the bottom of this map .	如果我們看看17世紀倫敦的倫敦地圖我們可以發現 , 穀物是從泰姆斯運河到達的而這張地圖的底部
so the grain markets were to the south of the city .	所以穀物市場就在城市的南方 。
and the roads leading up from them to cheapside , which was the main market , were also grain markets .	這條路從它們走到便宜的道路 , 也就是主要的市場 , 也是穀物市場 。
and if you look at the name of one of those streets , bread street , you can tell what was going on there 300 years ago .	如果你看那些街道的名字 , 麵包街 , 你可以看出三百年前的狀況 。
and the same of course was true for fish .	當然 , 魚也是如此 。
fish was , of course , coming in by river as well . same thing .	魚當然是從河裡運來的 。 同樣的事情 。
and of course billingsgate , famously , was london's fish market , operating onsite here until the mid1980s .	比林斯門 , 當時有名的倫敦的魚市場一直到1980年代中期都在使用
which is extraordinary , really , when you think about it .	想想看 , 這真的很不可思議 。
everybody else was wandering around with mobile phones that looked like bricks and sort of smelly fish happening down on the port .	其他每個人都在玩長得像磚塊的行動電話 , 還有在港口發生的臭魚 。
this is another thing about food in cities: once its roots into the city are established , they very rarely move .	城市裡食物的另一件事是:一旦食物的根部被建立起來 , 就很少會動 。
meat is a very different story because , of course , animals could walk into the city .	肉類是另外一個故事 , 因為 , 當然 , 動物們可以走進城市 。
so much of london's meat was coming from the northwest , from scotland and wales .	倫敦的大量肉品是從西北方來 , 來自蘇格蘭和威爾斯 。
so it was coming in , and arriving at the city at the northwest , which is why smithfield , london's very famous meat market , was located up there .	所以它來到倫敦的西北方 , 這就是為什麼史密斯菲爾德 , 倫敦著名的肉市場 , 位在那上面 。
poultry was coming in from east anglia and so on , to the northeast .	家禽類從東安格利亞進來 , 一直到東北方 。
i feel a bit like a weather woman doing this . anyway , and so the birds were coming in with their feet protected with little canvas shoes .	我覺得有點像氣象女人在做這件事 。 總之 , 鳥類也跟著進來 , 被小畫布保護著 。
and then when they hit the eastern end of cheapside , that's where they were sold , which is why it's called poultry .	一旦他們到達便宜的東邊 , 他們就被在那裡販賣 , 這就是所謂的 「 家禽 」 。
and , in fact , if you look at the map of any city built before the industrial age , you can trace food coming in to it .	實際上 , 如果你看任何城市的地圖在工業時代前建成 , 你可以追蹤進來的食物 。
you can actually see how it was physically shaped by food , both by reading the names of the streets , which give you a lot of clues .	你可以看到它實際上是如何被食物所塑造的 , 無論是通過閱讀街道的名字 , 可以給你很多線索 。
friday street , in a previous life , is where you went to buy your fish on a friday .	星期五街 , 在以前是你星期五去買魚的地方 。
but also you have to imagine it full of food .	你也必須想像它充滿了食物 。
because the streets and the public spaces were the only places where food was bought and sold .	因為街道和公共空間是唯一可以買到食物的地方 。
and if we look at an image of smithfield in 1830 you can see that it would have been very difficult to live in a city like this and be unaware of where your food came from .	如果我們看1830年的史密斯菲爾德的照片 , 你就會發現很難住在像這樣的城市 , 且不知你的食物從哪裡來 。
in fact , if you were having sunday lunch , the chances were it was mooing or bleating outside your window about three days earlier .	事實上 , 如果你有星期日午餐 , 你可能有三天前在你的窗外面舉行心情或出血 。
so this was obviously an organic city , part of an organic cycle .	所以這顯然是一個有機城市 , 是有機循環的一部分 。
and then 10 years later everything changed .	十年後 , 一切都改變了 。
this is an image of the great western in 1840 .	這是1840年大西部的照片 。
and as you can see , some of the earliest train passengers were pigs and sheep .	如你所見 , 最早的火車乘客當中有一些是豬和羊 。
so all of a sudden , these animals are no longer walking into market .	突然間 , 這些動物不再走進市場 。
they're being slaughtered out of sight and mind , somewhere in the countryside .	他們在眼睛和心智中被屠殺 , 在鄉間的某處 。
and they're coming into the city by rail .	他們是用鐵路運進城市的 。
and this changes everything .	這改變了一切 。
to start off with , it makes it possible for the first time to grow cities , really any size and shape , in any place .	首先 , 它讓它成為可能首次在任何地方種植任何大小和形狀 。
cities used to be constrained by geography ; they used to have to get their food through very difficult physical means .	過去城市會受到地理限制 ; 以前 , 城市得要透過很困難的物理手段來取得食物 。
all of a sudden they are effectively emancipated from geography .	突然間 , 它們就從地理釋放出來了 。
and as you can see from these maps of london , in the 90 years after the trains came , it goes from being a little blob that was quite easy to feed by animals coming in on foot , and so on , to a large splurge , that would be very , very difficult to feed with anybody on foot , either animals or people .	你可以從倫敦的地圖上看到在火車經過的九十年後倫敦的地圖從一個非常容易餵飽的小點變成一個非常大的小點 , 一個非常非常難餵飽任何人 , 無論是動物還是人 。
and of course that was just the beginning . after the trains came cars , and really this marks the end of this process .	當然這只是個開端 。 火車來了車之後 , 畫出了這整個過程的終點 。
it's the final emancipation of the city from any apparent relationship with nature at all .	它是城市中最後的解放 , 從大自然的任何明顯的關係中解放 。
and this is the kind of city that's devoid of smell , devoid of mess , certainly devoid of people , because nobody would have dreamed of walking in such a landscape .	這座城市沒有味道 , 更沒有混亂 , 當然也沒有人 , 因為從來沒有人夢想過能在這樣的風景中走路 。
in fact , what they did to get food was they got in their cars , drove to a box somewhere on the outskirts , came back with a week's worth of shopping , and wondered what on earth to do with it .	事實上 , 他們的做法是買到車 , 開車到郊區的某處一個箱子 , 帶回一週的購物 , 並想著要怎麼處理它 。
and this really is the moment when our relationship , both with food and cities , changes completely .	此時此刻 , 我們與食物及城市的關係都完全改變 。
here we have food that used to be the center , the social core of the city at the periphery .	以前我們有食物是市中心 , 城市的社會核心 , 在這邊的邊緣地帶 。
it used to be a social event , buying and selling food .	以前是社交活動 , 購買和賣食物 。
we used to cook ; now we just add water , or a little bit of an egg if you're making a cake or something .	我們以前會煮飯 , 現在只要加點水 , 或加一點點雞蛋 , 如果你要做蛋 , 或做些什麼 。
we don't smell food to see if it's okay to eat .	我們不會聞到食物 , 看看它有沒有好吃 。
we just read the back of a label on a packet .	我們只是看了包裝背後的標籤 。
and we don't value food . we don't trust it .	我們不珍惜食物 。 我們不信任它 。
so instead of trusting it , we fear it .	所以 , 我們不再信任它 , 我們害怕它 。
and instead of valuing it , we throw it away .	與其重視它 , 我們就把它拋諸腦後 。
one of the great ironies of modern food systems is that they've made the very thing they promised to make easier much harder .	現代食品系統最諷刺的一點是他們讓原本最容易做的東西變得更容易 。
by making it possible to build cities anywhere and any place , they've actually distanced us from our most important relationship , which is that of us and nature .	藉由它可以在任何地方、任何地方建立城市 , 它實際上使我們與我們最重要的關係保持距離 , 那就是我們和自然的關係 。
and also they've made us dependent on systems that only they can deliver , that , as we've seen , are unsustainable .	這也使得我們必須依賴這些只能提供的系統 , 如我們所見 , 這些系統是不可持續的 。
so what are we going to do about that ?	所以 , 我們要怎麼做 ?
it's not a new question .	這不是個新問題 。
500 years ago it's what thomas more was asking himself .	五百年前湯瑪斯.摩爾就在問他自己 。
this is the frontispiece of his book " utopia . "	這是他《烏托邦》這本書的前面畫 。
and it was a series of semiindependent citystates , if that sounds remotely familiar , a day's walk from one another where everyone was basically farmingmad , and grew vegetables in their back gardens , and ate communal meals together , and so on .	這是一系列半自給自足的城邦聽起來很熟悉每天走路每個人都在自家的後院種蔬菜然後一起享用餐點等等
and i think you could argue that food is a fundamental ordering principle of utopia , even though more never framed it that way .	我想 , 你可以說食物是烏托邦的基本原則即便摩爾最初是烏托邦的基本原則
and here is another very famous " utopian " vision , that of ebenezer howard , " the garden city . "	還有另外一個著名的烏托邦的視覺 , 伊伯內斯霍華的 " 田園城市 " 。
same idea: series of semiindependent citystates , little blobs of metropolitan stuff with arable land around , joined to one another by railway .	相同的概念:一系列的半自給自足的城邦 , 都市裡有些地方有農藥 , 用鐵路連接在一起 。
and again , food could be said to be the ordering principle of his vision .	食物可以再次地說是他視覺原理的指令
it even got built , but nothing to do with this vision that howard had .	甚至完成了 , 但與默斯克韋茲的這個願景沒有任何關係 。
and that is the problem with these utopian ideas , that they are utopian .	烏托邦理念的問題就在於它們是烏托邦
utopia was actually a word that thomas moore used deliberately .	烏托邦其實是湯瑪斯•摩爾刻意使用的詞 。
it was a kind of joke , because it's got a double derivation from the greek .	開個玩笑 , 因為希臘語有雙重導向
it can either mean a good place , or no place .	它可以是指一個好地方 , 或沒有地方 。
because it's an ideal . it's an imaginary thing . we can't have it .	因為它是理想的 。 它是想像的 。 我們無法擁有它 。
and i think , as a conceptual tool for thinking about the very deep problem of human dwelling , that makes it not much use .	我認為 , 一個概念性的工具 , 用來思考人類居住的深層問題 , 這就不太有用了 。
so i've come up with an alternative , which is sitopia , from the ancient greek , " sitos " for food , and " topos " for place .	所以我想出了一個替代方案 , 就是希托邦 , 來自古希臘文 , 「 希托 」 指的是食物 , 「 屁股 」 , 指定的地方 。
i believe we already live in sitopia .	我相信我們已經住在希托邦 。
we live in a world shaped by food , and if we realize that , we can use food as a really powerful tool a conceptual tool , design tool , to shape the world differently .	我們生活在由食物塑造的世界裡 , 如果我們意識到 , 我們可以用食物當作非常強大的工具 , 一個概念性的工具 , 設計工具 , 來改變世界 。
so if we were to do that , what might sitopia look like ?	所以如果我們這樣做 , 希托邦會長什麼樣子 ?
well i think it looks a bit like this .	嗯 , 我覺得看起來有點像這樣 。
i have to use this slide . it's just the look on the face of the dog .	我必須用這張投影片 。 這只是狗的臉 。
but anyway , this is it's food at the center of life , at the center of family life , being celebrated , being enjoyed , people taking time for it .	總之 , 它是生活的中心 , 在家庭生活的中心 , 被讚頌 , 樂在其中 , 人們花時間在做這件事 。
this is where food should be in our society .	食物就在我們的社會裡 。
but you can't have scenes like this unless you have people like this .	除非你有這些人 , 否則你不能有這樣的場景 。
by the way , these can be men as well .	順便一提 , 這也可以是男人 。
it's people who think about food , who think ahead , who plan , who can stare at a pile of raw vegetables and actually recognize them .	人們會想到食物 , 會預先思考 , 誰能計畫 , 盯著一堆生菜 , 實際認出它們 。
we need these people . we're part of a network .	我們需要這些人 , 我們是網路的一部分 。
because without these kinds of people we can't have places like this .	因為如果沒有這些人 , 我們就沒有這些地方 。
here , i deliberately chose this because it is a man buying a vegetable .	我故意選這張是因為這是男人在買蔬菜
but networks , markets where food is being grown locally .	但是網絡 , 食物在當地生長的市場 。
it's common . it's fresh .	很普遍 , 很新鮮 。
it's part of the social life of the city .	它是社交生活的一部分 。
because without that , you can't have this kind of place , food that is grown locally and also is part of the landscape , and is not just a zerosum commodity off in some unseen hellhole .	因為沒有了這些 , 你就不可能有這種地方、當地種植的食物 , 同時也是地景的一部分 , 且不只是在看不見的地獄裡 , 消費的商品 。
cows with a view .	牛則有自己的視角 。
steaming piles of humus .	冒著水泥的水堆
this is basically bringing the whole thing together .	這基本上是把整個東西結合在一起 。
and this is a community project i visited recently in toronto .	這是我最近在多倫多探訪的一個社區專案 。
it's a greenhouse , where kids get told all about food and growing their own food .	這是一間溫室 , 孩子們會全都跟食物有關 , 並自給自足 。
here is a plant called kevin , or maybe it's a plant belonging to a kid called kevin . i don't know .	這種植物叫做凱文 , 或說它是屬於凱文的孩子 , 我不知道 。
but anyway , these kinds of projects that are trying to reconnect us with nature is extremely important .	總之 , 這類計畫正試圖讓我們與大自然重新連結 , 是極其重要的 。
so sitopia , for me , is really a way of seeing .	所以 , 希托邦 , 對我來說 , 其實是一種看待的方式 。
it's basically recognizing that sitopia already exists in little pockets everywhere .	基本上 , 意識到希托邦已經存在於各地的小口袋中 。
the trick is to join them up , to use food as a way of seeing .	秘訣在於加入他們 , 運用食物作為一種觀點 。
and if we do that , we're going to stop seeing cities as big , metropolitan , unproductive blobs , like this .	如果我們這樣做 , 我們就會停止把城市視為是大的、城市的、沒生產力的區塊 , 像這樣 。
we're going to see them more like this , as part of the productive , organic framework of which they are inevitably a part , symbiotically connected .	我們會把它們看成是有生產力的有機架構的一部分 , 它們無可避免地被連結著 。
but of course , that's not a great image either , because we need not to be producing food like this anymore .	當然 , 這也不是很好的圖像 , 因為我們需要不再生產像這樣的食物 。
we need to be thinking more about permaculture , which is why i think this image just sums up for me the kind of thinking we need to be doing .	我們需要多思索永續農業 , 這就是為什麼我認為這張圖可以總結出我們該做的事 。
it's a reconceptualization of the way food shapes our lives .	它被重新概念化食物如何影響我們的生活 。
the best image i know of this is from 650 years ago .	我所知道的最好的圖像是650年前 。
it's ambrogio lorenzetti's " allegory of good government . "	安布洛吉歐•羅倫澤蒂的 " 良好政府的寓言 "
it's about the relationship between the city and the countryside .	重點是城市和鄉村之間的關係 。
and i think the message of this is very clear .	我想傳達給大家的訊息很清楚 。
if the city looks after the country , the country will look after the city .	如果城市照顧國家 , 國家會照顧城市 。
and i want us to ask now , what would ambrogio lorenzetti paint if he painted this image today ?	現在我想問大家安布洛吉歐•羅倫澤蒂會怎樣的顏料 ? 如果他現在畫這張圖呢 ?
what would an allegory of good government look like today ?	一個良好的政府的寓言會是什麼樣子的 ?
because i think it's an urgent question .	因為我認為這是一個緊迫的問題 。
it's one we have to ask , and we have to start answering .	這是我們必須問的 , 我們必須開始回答 。
we know we are what we eat .	我們知道我們吃什麼 。
we need to realize that the world is also what we eat .	我們需要了解 , 世界也是我們吃的東西 。
but if we take that idea , we can use food as a really powerful tool to shape the world better .	但如果我們採用這個點子 , 我們可以使用食物作為一個強大的工具 , 來改善這個世界 。
weeks from the charter for compassion launch , karen armstrong looks at religion's role in the 21st century: will its dogmas divide us ? or will it unite us for common good ? she reviews the catalysts that can drive the world's faiths to rediscover the golden rule .	同情憲章發佈數週 , 凱倫•阿姆斯壯在21世紀研究宗教角色:教條會分化我們嗎 ? 還是會再次審視讓世界的信仰重新找回信念來 , 重新找回教義 。
god , ted prize , global issues , politics , religion , tedglobal2009 , violence	上帝、ted大獎、全球議題、政治、宗教、tedglobal2009年的暴力 。
karen armstrong: let's revive the golden rule	karenarmstrong:讓我們重新審視黃金法則 。
for years i've been feeling frustrated , because as a religious historian , i've become acutely aware of the centrality of compassion in all the major world faiths .	多年來 , 我一直感到沮喪 , 因為身為宗教歷史學家 , 我敏銳地意識到慈悲的核心在世界上的主要宗教信仰 。
every single one of them has evolved their own version of what's been called the golden rule .	他們每個人都演化出自己的 " 黃金法則 " 版本 。
sometimes it comes in a positive version " always treat all others as you'd like to be treated yourself . "	有時候會出現一個正面的版本 「 人人都會對待自己 。 」
and equally important is the negative version " don't do to others what you would not like them to do to you . "	同樣重要的是負面的版本 「 不要對其他人做你不希望他們做的事情 。 」
look into your own heart , discover what it is that gives you pain and then refuse , under any circumstance whatsoever , to inflict that pain on anybody else .	看看你自己的內心 , 發現是什麼讓你有痛苦 , 然後拒絕各種情況下 , 以讓別人感受到痛苦 。
and people have emphasized the importance of compassion , not just because it sounds good , but because it works .	人們強調同情的重要性 , 不是因為它聽起來很棒 , 而是因為它很有效 。
people have found that when they have implemented the golden rule as confucius said , " all day and every day , " not just a question of doing your good deed for the day and then returning to a life of greed and egotism , but to do it all day and every day , you dethrone yourself from the center of your world , put another there , and you transcend yourself .	人們發現 , 當他們實施了黃金法則 , 就像孔子說: 「 一整天、每一天 」 , 不只是在做好事 , 接著又回到貪婪、自我主義的人生 , 但如果要做一整天 , 你就要脫離你世界的中心 , 另一條路你要超越自己 。
and it brings you into the presence of what's been called god , nirvana , rama , tao .	它會帶你進入所謂的 「 神 」 、 「 涅亞 」 、 「 道 」 的境界 。
something that goes beyond what we know in our egobound existence .	超越了我們對自我存在的了解 。
but you know you'd never know it a lot of the time , that this was so central to the religious life .	但你知道你不知道很多時候 , 這對於宗教生活來說是如此的重要 。
because with a few wonderful exceptions , very often when religious people come together , religious leaders come together , they're arguing about abstruse doctrines or uttering a council of hatred or inveighing against homosexuality or something of that sort .	因為有幾個美妙的例外 , 宗教人士聚集在一起 , 宗教領導人聚集在一起 , 他們爭論的是深奧的教義 , 或者說出一連串的仇恨 , 來對抗同性戀 , 或類似的事情 。
often people don't really want to be compassionate .	人們通常不想變得慈悲 。
i sometimes see when i'm speaking to a congregation of religious people a sort of mutinous expression crossing their faces because people often want to be right instead .	有時我會看到 , 當我和一群宗教人談話時 , 有點不太會用言語表達 , 因為人們通常會希望對的 。
and that of course defeats the object of the exercise .	這當然會打敗運動的目的 。
now why was i so grateful to ted ?	為何我對ted這麼感激 ?
because they took me very gently from my booklined study and brought me into the 21st century , enabling me to speak to a much , much wider audience than i could have ever conceived .	因為他們溫和地帶領我離開我的書房 , 帶我進入二十一世紀 , 讓我能和更廣的觀眾談話 , 遠超過我所能想像的範圍 。
because i feel an urgency about this .	因為我覺得這件事很迫切 。
if we don't manage to implement the golden rule globally , so that we treat all peoples , wherever and whoever they may be , as though they were as important as ourselves , i doubt that we'll have a viable world to hand on to the next generation .	如果我們不想辦法在全球執行黃金法則 , 不論誰來對待所有人 , 不論他們在哪裡 , 不論他們在哪裡 , 我懷疑我們會有一個可行的世界給下一代人 。
the task of our time , one of the great tasks of our time , is to build a global society , as i said , where people can live together in peace .	我們這個時代的任務 , 這個時代最大的一個任務 , 就是建立一個全球性社會 , 如我所說 , 讓人們可以和平共處 。
and the religions that should be making a major contribution are instead seen as part of the problem .	而應該對宗教做出重大貢獻的宗教反而被視為問題的一部分 。
and of course it's not just religious people who believe in the golden rule .	當然 , 不只是宗教人士 , 他們相信黃金法則 。
this is the source of all morality , this imaginative act of empathy , putting yourself in the place of another .	這是所有道德的源頭 , 這種富有想像力的同理心行為 , 讓自己置身於另一個地方 。
and so we have a choice , it seems to me .	所以我們有一個選擇 , 這對我來說 。
we can either go on bringing out or emphasizing the dogmatic and intolerant aspects of our faith , or we can go back to the rabbis . rabbi hillel , the older contemporary of jesus , who , when asked by a pagan to sum up the whole of jewish teaching while he stood on one leg , said , " that which is hateful to you , do not do to your neighbor .	我們可以繼續宣揚或強調宗教的教條或是不寬容的面向或者是我們可以回歸到拉比希爾 , 和耶穌當年老的那位祖母當他站在一條腿上說: 「 那對你來說是多麼美好的 , 而不是對你鄰居作出回應 。
that is the torah and everything else is only commentary . "	「 這就是教義 , 其他都只是評論 。 」
and the rabbis and the early fathers of the church who said that any interpretation of scripture that bred hatred and disdain was illegitimate .	猶太教和早期的父親們說任何對聖經的詮釋都是違法的
and we need to revive that spirit .	我們必須復興這樣的精神 。
and it's not just going to happen because a spirit of love wafts us down .	這不只因為愛的精神喚醒我們而發生 。
we have to make this happen , and we can do it with the modern communications that ted has introduced .	我們必須讓它實現 , 並且我們可以實現ted介紹的現代溝通 。
already i've been tremendously heartened at the response of all our partners .	我已經對所有伴侶的回應都大大地鼓舞著我 。
in singapore , we have a group going to use the charter to heal divisions recently that have sprung up in singaporean society , and some members of the parliament want to implement it politically .	在新加坡 , 我們有一組人要用憲章來治癒近期在新加坡社會出現的現象 , 議會的一些成員也想要採用政治手法 。
in malaysia , there is going to be an art exhibition in which leading artists are going to be taking people , young people , and showing them that compassion also lies at the root of all art .	在馬來西亞 , 將有一項藝術展覽將要帶領人們 , 年輕人 , 讓他們看見 , 慈悲其實也是所有藝術的根源 。
throughout europe , the muslim communities are holding events and discussions , are discussing the centrality of compassion in islam and in all faiths .	在歐洲各地 , 都有穆斯林團體舉辦事件和討論 , 討論伊斯蘭和所有信仰的核心 。
but it can't stop there . it can't stop with the launch .	但它不能就此停止 , 它不能就這樣跟著發射 。
religious teaching , this is where we've gone so wrong , concentrating solely on believing abstruse doctrines .	宗教教學 , 這才是我們做錯事的地方 , 非常專注於相信深奧的教義 。
religious teaching must always lead to action .	宗教教導必須永遠導致行動 。
and i intend to work on this till my dying day .	我打算在我的臨終日前工作 。
and i want to continue with our partners to do two things educate and stimulate compassionate thinking .	我還想繼續跟我們的夥伴做兩件事 , 教育並激發同情心思維 。
education because we've so dropped out of compassion .	教育是因為我們已經失去了同理心 。
people often think it simply means feeling sorry for somebody .	人們通常認為這只意味著對某些人感到遺憾 。
but of course you don't understand compassion if you're just going to think about it .	但想一想 , 你就是不懂慈悲 。
you also have to do it .	你也必須這樣做 。
i want them to get the media involved because the media are crucial in helping to dissolve some of the stereotypical views we have of other people , which are dividing us from one another .	我希望媒體參與其中 , 是因為媒體在協助我們破除一些我們對其他人有的刻板印象 , 將我們從彼此分離出來 。
the same applies to educators .	教育家也一樣 。
i'd like youth to get a sense of the dynamism , the dynamic and challenge of a compassionate lifestyle .	我希望青年能夠感受到一種動態主義 , 一種充滿同情心的生活型態和挑戰 。
and also see that it demands acute intelligence , not just a gooey feeling .	同時也要有智慧 , 不只是要有爛透了的感覺 。
i'd like to call upon scholars to explore the compassionate theme in their own and in other people's traditions .	我想請教學者來探索他們自己和其他人的傳統中慈悲的主題 。
and perhaps above all , to encourage a sensitivity about uncompassionate speaking , so that because people have this charter , whatever their beliefs or lack of them , they feel empowered to challenge uncompassionate speech , disdainful remarks from their religious leaders , their political leaders , from the captains of industry .	也許最重要的是培養對於沒有同情心的言論的敏感度 , 這麼一來 , 因為人們有這個憲章 , 不論他們的信仰或缺乏信仰 , 他們就會覺得有權力去挑戰沒有感情的言論 , 不確定的言論 , 來自他們宗教領袖、政治領袖 , 以及產業長官 。
because we can change the world , we have the ability .	因為我們能改變世界 , 我們有能力 。
i would never have thought of putting the charter online .	我從來不會想把特許放上網 。
i was still stuck in the old world of a whole bunch of boffins sitting together in a room and issuing yet another arcane statement .	我還被困在一個老世界裡 , 一群人坐在辦公室裡 , 發表了各種說法 。
and ted introduced me to a whole new way of thinking and presenting ideas .	ted介紹我一種全新的思考和呈現想法的方式 。
because that is what is so wonderful about ted .	這就是ted美妙的地方 。
in this room , all this expertise , if we joined it all together , we could change the world .	在這個房間裡 , 所有這些專業知識 , 如果我們能加入這間房間 , 我們就能改變世界 。
and of course the problems sometimes seem insuperable .	當然 , 有些時候 , 這些問題似乎很容易解決 。
but i'd just like to quote , finish at the end with a reference to a british author , an oxford author whom i don't quote very often , c . s . lewis .	但我想引用一句話來結束 , 關於一位英國的作者 , 一位牛津的作家 , 我不太常提到他 , c.s.路易斯 。
but he wrote one thing that stuck in my mind ever since i read it when i was a schoolgirl .	但他寫下的一句話令我印象深刻 , 就在我還是個學童時期的心中 。
it's in his book " the four loves . "	這是他《四項愛》的書 。
he said that he distinguished between erotic love , when two people gaze , spellbound , into each other's eyes .	他說 , 他區分情愛 , 當兩個人凝視、拼字 , 彼此的眼睛 ,
and then he compared that to friendship , when two people stand side by side , as it were , shoulder to shoulder , with their eyes fixed on a common goal .	接著他把這感情和友誼做比較 , 當兩個人站在一起 , 肩並肩 , 視力固定在一個共同的目標上 。
we don't have to fall in love with each other , but we can become friends .	我們不需要愛上彼此 , 但我們可以成為朋友 。
and i am convinced .	我是被說服的 。
i felt it very strongly during our little deliberations at vevey , that when people of all different persuasions come together , working side by side for a common goal , differences melt away .	在我們對薇薇的思考期間 , 我很強烈地感受到 , 當不同說法的人集合在一起 , 一同合作為共同的目標努力時 , 差異就會消失 。
and we learn amity .	我們懂得正義 。
and we learn to live together and to get to know one another .	我們學習彼此住在一起 , 了解彼此 。
thank you very much .	非常謝謝 。
